<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Product_Endorsements">Product
Endorsements</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14"
title="Edit
section:
Product
Endorsements">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Underwood
has
had
many
endorsements
throughout
her
career.
She
has
signed
multimillion
dollar
deals
with
Sketchers,
Target,
Nintendo,
Olay
and
Nicole
by
OPI.
In
2005,
Underwood
appeared
in
<a
href="/wiki/Sketchers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sketchers"
class="mw-redirect">Sketchers</a>
global
advertising
campaign.
In
2008,
Underwood
worked
with
<a
href="/wiki/Nintendo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nintendo">Nintendo</a>
for
the
launch
of
their
<a
href="/wiki/Nintendo_DS?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nintendo
DS">Nintendo
DS</a>
appearing
in
various
television
commercials.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_DS_250-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_DS-250"><span>[</span>250<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2007,
Underwood
appeared
in
Target
advertisements
promoting
her
album
Carnival
Ride.
The
limited
edition
of
the
album
which
included
a
behind
the
scenes
DVD
was
exclusively
sold
at
Target.<sup
id="cite_ref-251"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-251"><span>[</span>251<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2008,
Underwood
became
the
spokesperson
for
<a
href="/wiki/Vitamin_Water?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Vitamin
Water"
class="mw-redirect">Vitamin
Water</a>
appearing
in
television
and
magazine
advertisements.
Underwood
also
hosts
a
guide
to
a
healthy
lifestyle
on
Vitamin
Water's
website.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Vitamin_Water_252-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Vitamin_Water-252"><span>[</span>252<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2010,
Underwood
became
the
spokesperson
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/Pedigree_Petfoods?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pedigree
Petfoods">Pedigree</a>
adoption
drive.
In
2011,
she
became
the
first
celebrity
brand
ambassador
for
<a
href="/wiki/Olay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Olay">Olay</a>
skin
care.
Underwood
has
appeared
in
the
global
advertising
campaign
for
their
facial
wash.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Olay_253-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Olay-253"><span>[</span>253<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
January
2014,
Underwood
signed
a
deal
with
Nicole
by
OPI
to
launch
14
new
nail
lacquers.
The
collection
features
a
colorful
mosaic
of
hues
in
a
variety
of
finishes,
including
pink,
red
and
coral
cr&egrave;mes;
chunky
and
textured
glitters
in
gold,
silver
and
white;
and
rich
eggplant
and
khaki
green
shades.
&quot;Carrie
is
the
perfect
partner
for
Nicole
by
OPI.
Her
music
evokes
powerful
emotions
in
its
listeners,
and
we
wanted
to
give
fans
a
way
to
express
their
feelings
through
color,&quot;
explained
Suzi
Weiss-Fischmann,
Nicole
by
OPI
Executive
VP
&amp;
Artistic
Director.
&quot;In
working
closely
with
Carrie,
we
came
up
with
14
nail
lacquers
that
truly
encapsulate
her
soulful
spirit
and
showcase
different
facets
of
her
personality
–
from
softer
pastels
and
dark
sultry
shades
to
playful
glitters.&quot;
<sup
id="cite_ref-254"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-254"><span>[</span>254<span>]</span></a></sup>
That
same
month,
Almay
announced
Underwood
had
signed
a
deal
to
serve
as
Almay's
global
brand
ambassador.
She
appeared
in
TV
and
print
advertisements
later
that
month.
<sup
id="cite_ref-255"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-255"><span>[</span>255<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
has
mentioned
plans
of
designing
a
line
of
clothing
and
accessories.
Fashion
designer
Tommy
Hilfiger
endorsed
the
idea,
saying
Underwood
is
one
the
best
in
music
when
it
comes
to
creating
images
through
fashion.<sup
id="cite_ref-256"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-256"><span>[</span>256<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Philanthropy">Philanthropy</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15"
title="Edit
section:
Philanthropy">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Underwood
established
the
Checotah
Animal,
Town,
and
School
Foundation
in
2009.
The
foundation
helps
with
general
causes,
needs
and
services
in
the
area
of
Checotah
to
directly
impact
the
community.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Chairty_257-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Chairty-257"><span>[</span>257<span>]</span></a></sup>
&quot;My
hometown
is
extremely
supportive
of
me
and
I
feel
blessed
to
be
able
to
create
something
as
a
way
of
giving
back;
to
say
thank
you,&quot;
said
Underwood.<sup
id="cite_ref-CATS_258-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-CATS-258"><span>[</span>258<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_philanthropy_259-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_philanthropy-259"><span>[</span>259<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
is
a
supporter
of
arts
education.
In
2009,
Underwood’s
foundation
&quot;Checotah
Animal,
Town
&amp;
School
Foundation&quot;
and
the
<a
href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Academy
of
Country
Music">Academy
of
Country
Music</a>
foundation
&quot;ACM
Lifting
Lives&quot;
partnered
to
give
students
in
Checotah,
Oklahoma
a
gift
valued
at
more
than
$120,000
in
new
instruments
for
their
music
programs.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Arts_260-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Arts-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup>
Underwood
held
a
surprise
concert
at
a
local
high
school
and
then
unveiled
the
gifts.
The
instruments
will
be
shared
throughout
the
Checotah
school
district,
and
were
ordered
through
Yamaha
Corporate
Artist
Affairs
at
a
special
philanthropic
price.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Arts_260-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Arts-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Arts_260-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Arts-260"><span>[</span>260<span>]</span></a></sup>
During
the
2011
holiday
season,
her
foundation
donated
$350,000
to
the
Checotah
schools.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Donation_261-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Donation-261"><span>[</span>261<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
is
a
supporter
of
animal
rights.
Underwood
is
a
supporter
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Humane_Society_of_the_United_States?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Humane
Society
of
the
United
States"
class="mw-redirect">Humane
Society
of
the
United
States</a>
(HSUS)
and
has
done
several
public
service
announcements
for
the
organization.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_HSUS_262-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_HSUS-262"><span>[</span>262<span>]</span></a></sup>
Underwood
has
also
done
a
&quot;Protect
Your
Pets&quot;
<a
href="/wiki/Public_service_announcement?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Public
service
announcement">public
service
announcement</a>
for
<a
href="/wiki/Do_Something?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Do
Something">Do
Something</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_PSA_263-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_PSA-263"><span>[</span>263<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2010,
Underwood
became
the
official
spokesperson
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/Pedigree_Petfoods?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pedigree
Petfoods">Pedigree</a>
adoption
drive.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_Pedigree_264-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_Pedigree-264"><span>[</span>264<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
March
29,
2010
Underwood
and
Pedigree
partnered
to
donate
$10,000
to
a
New
York
City
Animal
Shelter.
In
April
2011,
Underwood
opened
the
Happy
Paws
Animal
Shelter
in
her
hometown.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_Shelter_265-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_Shelter-265"><span>[</span>265<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
January
10,
2012,
it
was
reported,
but
had
previously
been
blogged
by
Underwood
herself
on
her
official
fan-site,
that
the
singer
rescued
an
abandoned
dog
along
highway.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_saves_dogs_266-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_saves_dogs-266"><span>[</span>266<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
and
her
husband
made
a
video
for
the
&quot;Do
It
for
Daron&quot;
campaign
urging
young
people
to
stop
bullying.<sup
id="cite_ref-Stop_Bullying_267-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Stop_Bullying-267"><span>[</span>267<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
July
2012,
she
publicly
endorsed
same-sex
marriage.
She
told
the
British
newspaper
<i>The
Independent</i>,
&quot;As
a
married
person
myself,
I
don't
know
what
it's
like
to
be
told
I
can't
marry
somebody
I
love,
and
want
to
marry,&quot;
she
said.
&quot;I
can't
imagine
how
that
must
feel.
I
definitely
think
we
should
all
have
the
right
to
love,
and
love
publicly,
the
people
that
we
want
to
love.&quot;
Underwood
went
on
to
say,
&quot;Our
church
is
gay
friendly.
Above
all,
God
wanted
us
to
love
others.
It's
not
about
setting
rules,
or
[saying]
'everyone
has
to
be
like
me'.
No.
We're
all
different.
That's
what
makes
us
special.
We
have
to
love
each
other
and
get
on
with
each
other.
It's
not
up
to
me
to
judge
anybody.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-268"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-268"><span>[</span>268<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
launched
the
<a
href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Academy
of
Country
Music">Academy
of
Country
Music</a>
Lifting
Lives
Temporary
Home
Fund
in
2010.
The
Fund
specifically
benefits
victims
of
the
Tennessee
floods
of
early
2010
and
it
was
kicked
off
with
grants
that
Underwood
received
from
ACM
as
Entertainer
of
the
Year.
She
also
teamed
up
with
Brooks
and
Dunn
to
support
the
new
Fund
by
recording
a
<a
href="/wiki/Public_Service_Announcement?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Public
Service
Announcement"
class="mw-redirect">Public
Service
Announcement</a>
(PSA).<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_donation_269-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_donation-269"><span>[</span>269<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
is
involved
with
a
number
of
organizations
that
benefit
children.
In
January
2010,
she
partnered
with
Country
Cares
for
St.
Jude
Kids
visiting
the
<a
href="/wiki/St._Jude_Children%27s_Research_Hospital?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="St.
Jude
Children's
Research
Hospital">St.
Jude
Children's
Research
Hospital</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_st_jude_270-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_st_jude-270"><span>[</span>270<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
February
2011,
Underwood
donated
$140,125
to
<a
href="/wiki/Save_the_Children?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Save
the
Children">Save
the
Children</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_Save_the_Children_271-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_Save_the_Children-271"><span>[</span>271<span>]</span></a></sup>
This
charitable
initiative
was
inspired
by
the
&quot;36
cents&quot;
written
in
the
lyrics
of
Underwood's
album
track
&quot;Change&quot;
on
her
album
<i>Play
On</i>,
which
addresses
how
even
the
smallest
bit
of
spare
change
that
one
might
have
can
add
up
to
make
a
difference
and
help
&quot;change&quot;
the
world.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_36_272-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_36-272"><span>[</span>272<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Underwood
is
a
supporter
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/United_Service_Organization?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="United
Service
Organization"
class="mw-redirect">United
Service
Organization</a>,
Clothes
off
our
back,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Habitat_For_Humanity?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Habitat
For
Humanity"
class="mw-redirect">Habitat
For
Humanity</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Carrie_Underwood_giving_273-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Carrie_Underwood_giving-273"><span>[</span>273<span>]</span></a></sup>
To
benefit
<a
href="/wiki/Cancer_research?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cancer
research">cancer
research</a>,
in
August
2008
Underwood
joined
<a
href="/wiki/Beyonc%C3%A9?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Beyonc&eacute;">Beyonc&eacute;</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Mariah_Carey?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mariah
Carey">Mariah
Carey</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Mary_J._Blige?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mary
J.
Blige">Mary
J.
Blige</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Miley_Cyrus?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Miley
Cyrus">Miley
Cyrus</a>
and
other
female
artists
to
record
the
song
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Just_Stand_Up!?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Just
Stand
Up!">Just
Stand
Up!</a>&quot;.
The
proceeds
benefited
<a
href="/wiki/Stand_Up_to_Cancer?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stand
Up
to
Cancer">Stand
Up
to
Cancer</a>
(SU2C).
As
a
result
of
their
fund
raising
efforts,
the
SU2C
scientific
advisory
committee,
overseen
by
the
<a
href="/wiki/American_Association_for_Cancer_Research?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="American
Association
for
Cancer
Research">American
Association
for
Cancer
Research</a>
was
able
to
award
$73.6
million
towards
novel,
groundbreaking
research.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_SU2C_274-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_SU2C-274"><span>[</span>274<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
song
peaked
at
number
eleven
on
<i>Billboard</i>'s
Hot
100
Songs.</p>








<p>In
May
2012,
Underwood
announced
that
she
would
donate
$1
of
every
ticket
sold
on
<a
href="/wiki/Blown_Away_Tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blown
Away
Tour">Blown
Away
Tour</a>
to
the
<a
href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="American
Red
Cross">American
Red
Cross</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Underwood_Red_Cross_Donation_275-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Underwood_Red_Cross_Donation-275"><span>[</span>275<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
May
24,
2013,
Underwood
announced
that
she
would
be
donating
$1
million
in
proceeds
from
her
recent
Blown
Away
Tour
to
the
Red
Cross
for
relief
efforts
in
response
to
the
Oklahoma
tornado.
&quot;I
have
watched
the
devastation
in
my
home
state
of
Oklahoma
over
the
past
several
days
with
great
sadness,&quot;
Underwood
said
in
a
statement.
&quot;With
the
help
of
my
fans
who
attended
my
concerts
over
the
past
year,
we
can
offer
the
Red
Cross
a
little
extra
help
in
comforting
those
affected
by
the
recent
tornados.&quot;
Neal
Litvack,
chief
development
officer
for
the
Red
Cross,
said,
&quot;The
impact
of
the
tornados
in
Oklahoma
and
the
Midwest
was
devastating
and
the
road
to
recovery
will
be
long
for
many
families.
Through
the
generosity
of
Carrie,
the
American
Red
Cross
can
quickly
respond
with
shelter,
food
and
comfort
now,
and
with
lasting
help
as
they
move
toward
recovery.&quot;</p>

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Awards">Awards</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Carrie_Underwood&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19"
title="Edit
section:
Awards">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<div
class="rellink
relarticle
mainarticle">








Main
article:









<a
href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Carrie_Underwood?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="List
of
awards
and
nominations
received
by
Carrie
Underwood">List
of
awards
and
nominations
received
by
Carrie
Underwood</a>







</div>








<p>Underwood
has
been
the
recipient
of
six
<a
href="/wiki/Grammy_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grammy
Award">Grammy
Awards</a>,
seven
<a
href="/wiki/American_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="American
Music
Awards"
class="mw-redirect">American
Music
Awards</a>,
five
<a
href="/wiki/Country_Music_Association_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Country
Music
Association
Awards">Country
Music
Association
Awards</a>,
ten
<a
href="/wiki/Academy_of_Country_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Academy
of
Country
Music
Awards">Academy
of
Country
Music
Awards</a>,
and
sixteen
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_Music_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
Music
Awards"
class="mw-redirect">Billboard
Music
Awards</a>.
Underwood
was
inducted
into
the
Grand
Ole
Opry
in
2008
for
her
many
accomplishments
in
country
music.
Additionally,
she
has
received
one
<a
href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Golden
Globe
Award">Golden
Globe
Award</a>
nomination.</p>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Carrie_Underwood&page=1&ac=24&qid=550F823BF1947AEE3C2B33549BEBFE31&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>

<h2

</h2>







<p
class="ur">
<span
class="grey
b
valign">A:</span>
<span
class="qna-txt">
Carrie
Underwood
was
born
on
March
10,
1983
in
Checotah,
Oklahoma.
Carrie
stands
5'
4&quot;
tall,
has
green
eyes
and
blond
hair.
Carrie
is
a
practicing
vegetarian.
<a
id="r1_t"
